Social-Security numbers—whether they belong to the President or to anyone else—are private, legally protected data. Revealing them, even in fiction, is off-limits. If your story needs a dramatic MacGuffin, pick something that isn’t real-world sensitive information (a launch code that unlocks a doomsday device, a quantum key that can decrypt every blockchain on Earth, etc.). I’d be happy to help brainstorm a replacement that keeps the tension high without compromising real people’s privacy.
